Marty McFlyin's Ortho Deck::2) Pocket Pimped::01 The Basics::01.01 X-rays::Upper Extremity	What <u>radiographic finding</u>&nbsp;on <u>AP view</u>&nbsp;is suggestive of a <b>posterior shoulder dislocation</b>?<div><br></div><div>{{c1::Light bulb sign}}</div>	"<div>Normal is on bottom left of 1st picture. Marty McFlyin's Ortho Deck::2) Pocket Pimped::01 The Basics::01.01 X-rays::Upper Extremity	What <u>view</u> is a <u>true AP</u> of the <b>glenohumeral joint</b>?<div><br></div><div>{{c1::Grashey}}</div>	"This is considered a ""true AP"" view since the view is AP to the scapula instead of AP to the patient. The view is obtained with the patient rotated 35-45 degrees and his/her scapular body up against the imaging detector.<div><br></div><div><b>G</b>rashey = <b>G</b>lenohumeral<br><div><div><br></div><div><img src=""Screen Shot 2020-05-02 at 10.54.52 AM.png""><br></div></div></div>"																Alexortho::pimped PocketPimped TheBasics UpperExtremity Xrays

Marty McFlyin's Ortho Deck::2) Pocket Pimped::01 The Basics::01.01 X-rays::Upper Extremity	The <b>sternoclavicular (SC) joint</b> is best visualized on what view?<div><br></div><div>{{c1::Serendipity}}</div>	"<div>SC dislocations are rare. <b>Anterior</b>&nbsp;occurs <u>more often</u> than <b>posterior</b>. Complications include pneumothorax, SVC laceration, subclavian artery/vein occlusion, or tracheal rupture. CT scan will establish the diagnosis.</div><div><br></div><img src=""seren.jpg"">"																PocketPimped TheBasics UpperExtremity Xrays
Marty McFlyin's Ortho Deck::2) Pocket Pimped::01 The Basics::01.01 X-rays::Upper Extremity	A <b>Hill-Sachs</b>&nbsp;lesion is <u>best visualized</u>&nbsp;on what view?<div><br></div><div>{{c1::Stryker Notch}}</div>	"<div><b>Hill-Sachs</b> occurs <u>during anterior dislocation</u> when the <u>anterior rim of the glenoid</u> causes a <u>depression in the posterolateral head</u> of humerus. <b>Stryker Notch</b>&nbsp;view allows for easy visualization of the cortical depression.</div><div><br></div><img src=""pathophysiology-mechanism-hillsachs-radiology-lesions-original.png""><div><div><img src=""Screen Shot 2020-05-02 at 11.31.21 AM.png""><br></div></div>"																PocketPimped TheBasics UpperExtremity Xrays
